中文摘要：气候与环境决策日益需要在异构输入之间进行推理，包括网格化物理数据、卫星图像、地理空间背景和模拟器输出。天气与气候基础模型能够很好地进行预测，但无法以语言进行交互式推理；而大型语言模型（LLM）能以语言进行推理，但无法直接操作高维地球系统数据。因此，地球科学中的真实科学工作流尚未得到充分服务。我们提出了TerraBench，一个用于基于地球科学推理的基准测试，它建立在TerraAgent之上，TerraAgent是一个ReAct风格的可执行框架，交错进行推理、工具调用和观察，将LLM规划与环境检索、地理空间处理、模拟以及人工制品支持计算等科学工具相结合。TerraBench在单一可执行接口中统一了地球观测图像、网格化数据、GIS推理和模拟的分析，而之前的基准测试将这些能力隔离到狭窄的单独任务中。它也是该领域中首个将过程级工具使用指标与容差感知数值评分相结合的工作。该基准包含403个广泛的智能体任务，分布在三个轨道（基础、模拟器基础和文档基础验证）和八个应用领域，共24500个经过验证的执行步骤。这些结果表明，可靠的地球科学智能体必须超越工具访问，协调异构工作流，精确参数化工具，并保留人工制品来源。

Original abstract: Climate and environmental decision-making increasingly requires reasoning across heterogeneous inputs, including gridded physical data, satellite imagery, geospatial context, and simulator outputs. Weather and climate foundation models can forecast well, but do not reason interactively in language, while large language models (LLMs) reason in language but cannot operate directly on high-dimensional Earth-system data. As a result, real scientific workflows in Earth-science remain underserved. We introduce TerraBench, a benchmark for grounded Earth-science reasoning, built on TerraAgent, a ReAct-style executable framework that interleaves reasoning, tool calls, and observations to couple LLM planning with scientific tools for environmental retrieval, geospatial processing, simulation, and artifact-backed computation. TerraBench unifies analysis of Earth observation imagery, gridded data, GIS reasoning and simulation in a single executable interface, whereas prior benchmarks isolate these capabilities into narrow individual tasks. It is also the first in this space to pair process-level tool-use metrics with tolerance-aware numeric scoring. The benchmark comprises 403 extensive agentic tasks across three tracks (Fundamentals, Simulator-Grounded, and Document-Grounded Verification) and eight application domains with 24,500 verified execution steps. These results indicate that reliable Earth-science agents must go beyond tool access to coordinate heterogeneous workflows, parameterize tools precisely, and preserve artifact provenance.

### [32] [ARMOR-MAD: Adaptive Routing for Heterogeneous Multi-Agent Debate in Large Language Model Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13197v1)
*Fuqiang Niu,Bowen Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自适应多agent辩论推理框架，通用多agent协作方法。

TL;DR: 提出ARMOR-MAD，一种无需训练的异质多智能体辩论框架，通过条件计算和一致性控制提升推理准确性和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固定辩论流程浪费计算资源且放大相关错误，需要更高效的动态辩论机制。

Method: 结合三个组件：PAR决定是否需要辩论，EASE动态停止辩论，SOD降低异常答案权重。

Result: 在MATH Level 5、GSM8K、MMLU和MMLU-Pro上，ARMOR-MAD分别达到65.5%、96.5%、90.0%和81.5%的准确率，优于固定轮次异质辩论。

Conclusion: 模型异质性和一致性控制对MAD的准确性和效率都很重要。

中文摘要：多智能体辩论（MAD）可以提升大型语言模型的推理能力，但固定的辩论流程往往浪费计算资源，并可能放大相似智能体之间的相关性错误。我们提出ARMOR-MAD，一个无需训练的异质MAD框架，将辩论视为条件计算。ARMOR-MAD结合了三个组件：辩论前一致性路由（PAR）决定独立生成的Round-0答案是否需要辩论；早期一致停止评估器（EASE）在收敛后停止辩论；语义异常检测（SOD）在聚合过程中降低异常最终答案的权重。在MATH Level 5、GSM8K、MMLU和MMLU-Pro上，ARMOR-MAD始终优于使用相同模型池的固定轮次异质辩论，分别达到65.5%、96.5%、90.0%和81.5%的准确率。结果表明，真正的模型异质性和基于一致性的控制对于使MAD更准确和高效都至关重要。

Original abstract: Multi-agent debate (MAD) can improve large language model reasoning, but fixed debate pipelines often waste computation and can amplify correlated errors among similar agents. We propose ARMOR-MAD, a training-free heterogeneous MAD framework that treats debate as conditional computation. ARMOR-MAD combines three components: Pre-debate Agreement Routing (PAR) decides whether independently generated Round-0 answers require debate; Early Agreement Stopping Evaluator (EASE) stops debate after convergence; and Semantic Outlier Detection (SOD) down-weights abnormal final answers during aggregation. Across MATH Level 5, GSM8K, MMLU, and MMLU-Pro, ARMOR-MAD consistently improves over fixed-round heterogeneous debate with the same model pool, reaching 65.5\%, 96.5\%, 90.0\%, and 81.5\% accuracy, respectively. The results suggest that genuine model heterogeneity and agreement-based control are both important for making MAD more accurate and efficient.

### [33] [LLM-as-an-Investigator: Evidence-First Reasoning for Robust Interactive Problem Diagnosis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13220v1)
*Fabrizio Marozzo,Pietro Liò*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 证据优先的agent诊断框架，可迁移至代码调试等coding agent任务。

TL;DR: 本文提出LLM-as-an-Investigator方法，通过证据优先的问题诊断代理，有效减少用户驱动的谄媚行为，提升技术问题诊断准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决LLM在交互中过早接受用户假设导致错误诊断的问题。

Method: 提出LLM-as-an-Investigator方法，通过解决方案调查代理，估计问题模糊性、生成候选假设、提出澄清问题并更新概率，直到证据足够支持唯一假设。

Result: 在机械、电气和液压领域的已解决技术论坛基准上，所提方法比直接提示和仅推理基线更准确地识别问题，并减少了用户引起的对话偏差。

Conclusion: 证据优先的协议有助于实现稳健的问题诊断，降低用户驱动的谄媚影响。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被用作技术问题解决的交互式助手。然而，当用户提供不完整的描述或似是而非但未经证实的解释时，LLM可能会过早地认同这些假设，并在收集足够证据之前提出解决方案。我们将这种行为称为用户驱动的谄媚：LLM倾向于强化用户提供的假设，而不是测试替代解释。本文介绍了LLM-as-an-Investigator，一种基于证据优先的自主AI方法论，用于稳健的问题诊断。该方法通过一个解决方案调查代理实现，该代理估计初始问题描述的模糊性，生成候选假设，提出有针对性的澄清问题，并在每次回答后更新假设概率。代理不会立即产生响应，而是继续调查，直到证据使某个候选解释强于其他替代方案。为了评估该方法，我们构建了一个来自机械、电气和液压领域已解决技术论坛帖子的基准。我们使用一个三代理评估管道，其中问题-解决方案提取代理将已解决的帖子转换为结构化案例，真实答案评估代理模拟用户但隐藏已知解决方案，被测助手尝试通过对话恢复解决方案。实验比较了标准助手、推理导向LLM和基于调查的模型在不同的LLM骨干上。除了诊断准确性外，我们还分析了标准助手如何在诊断案例中遵循误导性的用户假设。结果表明，所提出的方法比直接提示和仅推理基线更准确地识别问题，而其基于证据的协议有助于减少用户引起的对话偏差。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used as interactive assistants for technical problem solving. However, when users provide incomplete descriptions or plausible but unverified explanations, LLMs may prematurely align with these assumptions and propose solutions before collecting sufficient evidence. We refer to this behavior as user-driven sycophancy: the tendency of an LLM to reinforce a user-provided hypothesis instead of testing alternative explanations. This paper introduces LLM-as-an-Investigator, an evidence-first agentic AI methodology for robust problem diagnosis. The approach is implemented through a Solution Investigator Agent, which estimates the ambiguity of an initial problem description, generates candidate hypotheses, asks targeted clarification questions, and updates hypothesis probabilities after each answer. Rather than producing an immediate response, the agent continues the investigation until the evidence makes one candidate explanation stronger than the alternatives. To evaluate the approach, we build a benchmark from solved technical forum threads in mechanical, electrical, and hydraulic domains. We use a three-agent evaluation pipeline in which a Problem-Solution Extractor Agent converts solved threads into structured cases, a Ground-Truth Evaluator Agent simulates the user while hiding the known solution, and the tested assistant attempts to recover the solution through dialogue. The experiments compare standard assistants, reasoning-oriented LLMs, and the proposed investigator-based model across LLM backbones. In addition to diagnostic accuracy, we analyze how standard assistants follow misleading user hypotheses in diagnostic cases. The results show that the proposed approach identifies the problem more accurately than direct prompting and reasoning-only baselines, while its evidence-first protocol helps reduce user-induced conversational bias.

</details>


### [34] [TwinBI: An Agentic Digital Twin for Efficient Augmented Interactions with Business Intelligence Dashboards](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13731v1)
*Jisoo Jang Wen-Syan Li*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: BI仪表盘的agent数字孪生框架，通用agent状态管理可迁移。

TL;DR: TwinBI通过数字孪生框架统一LLM智能体与BI仪表板状态，显著提升多步分析的一致性和准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多步分析中，仪表板直接操作与LLM自然语言查询模式不同步，导致分析状态难以保持一致。

Method: 提出TwinBI框架，结合LLM智能体系统与可执行的BI仪表板状态，通过统一交互日志重建共享分析状态，并暴露模式视图、SQL、日志和/insights命令等工件。

Result: 在A/B测试中，精确匹配准确率从43.3%提升至63.3%，部分匹配准确率从48.3%提升至70.8%，超时率从40.0%降至10.0%；可用性研究中用户任务准确率高、工作负载中等。

Conclusion: TwinBI通过将仪表板状态转化为可操作上下文，同时提高了智能体分析可靠性和用户分析支持。

中文摘要：商业智能（BI）日益将仪表板交互与基于LLM的辅助相结合，但这两种模式在多步分析过程中常常不同步。当用户在直接仪表板操作和自然语言查询之间切换时，很难在过滤器、层级、指标和图表上下文中保持一致的分析状态。我们提出了TwinBI，一种基于智能体的数字孪生框架，它将基于LLM的智能体系统与可执行的BI仪表板状态相结合。TwinBI通过从统一交互日志重建的共享分析状态，统一了对话交互、仪表板操作、语义基础与溯源追踪。它还暴露了诸如模式视图、SQL、日志以及用于基于状态的分析摘要的/insights命令等工件。我们通过两种互补方式评估TwinBI。在相同骨干智能体的受控A/B基准测试中，与仅仪表板相比，TwinBI将精确匹配准确率从43.3%提升至63.3%，部分匹配准确率从48.3%提升至70.8%，并将超时率从40.0%大幅降低至10.0%。在可用性研究中，参与者受益于集成的仪表板与聊天工作流，实现了高任务准确率、中等工作负载以及对状态感知交互机制的有利评价。这些结果表明，TwinBI通过将可见的仪表板状态转化为更丰富的可操作上下文，提高了智能体级别的分析可靠性和面向用户的分析支持。我们的数据集和源代码可在以下网址获取：https://github.com/simonjisu/TwinBI

Original abstract: Business intelligence (BI) increasingly combines dashboard interaction with LLM-based assistance, but these two modes often fall out of sync during multi-step analysis. As users switch between direct dashboard manipulation and natural-language queries, it becomes difficult to preserve a consistent analytical state across filters, hierarchies, metrics, and chart context. We present TwinBI, an agentic digital-twin framework that couples an LLM-based agent system with an executable BI dashboard state. TwinBI unifies conversational interaction, dashboard manipulation, semantic grounding, and provenance tracking through a shared analytical state reconstructed from a unified interaction log. It also exposes artifacts such as schema views, SQL, logs, and an /insights command for state-grounded analytical summaries. We evaluate TwinBI in two complementary ways. In a controlled A/B benchmark with the same backbone agent, TwinBI improves exact-match accuracy from 43.3% to 63.3%, partial-credit accuracy from 48.3% to 70.8%, and substantially reduces timeout rate from 40.0% to 10.0% relative to Dashboard alone. In a usability study, participants benefited from the integrated dashboard-and-chat workflow, with high task accuracy, moderate workload, and favorable ratings for state-aware interaction mechanisms. These results suggest that TwinBI improves both agent-level analytical reliability and user-facing analytical support by turning visible dashboard state into richer actionable context. Our dataset and source code are available at: https://github.com/simonjisu/TwinBI

</details>


### [35] [From Verdict to Process: Agentic Reinforcement Learning for Multi-Stage Fact Verification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13262v1)

TL;DR: ProFact是一个基于智能体强化学习的框架，通过过程感知奖励进行端到端优化，有效协调多阶段事实核查的各个步骤，显著提升性能与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出ProFact，一种智能体强化学习框架，训练统一的策略来协调声明分解、证据寻求、答案生成和判决预测，并引入过程感知奖励以提供阶段级学习信号。

Original abstract: Recent approaches combining Large Language Models (LLMs) with retrieval-augmented reasoning have shown promise for automated fact verification. To process complex claims, these verification pipelines typically execute multi-stage workflows that coordinate tightly coupled modules, including claim decomposition, evidence gathering, and verdict prediction. However, existing methods optimize individual stages in isolation or rely on fixed heuristics, which limits adaptive coordination among stages and can lead to suboptimal outcomes. In this work, we propose ProFact, an agentic reinforcement learning framework for end-to-end optimization of multi-stage fact verification trajectories. ProFact trains a unified policy to coordinate claim decomposition, evidence seeking, answer generation, and verdict prediction. To address the sparse and delayed supervision provided by final veracity labels, ProFact introduces process-aware rewards that provide stage-level learning signals throughout the verification process. Empirical evaluation shows that ProFact consistently outperforms strong baselines in both verification performance and inference efficiency. These results highlight the effectiveness of process-aware trajectory optimization for multi-stage fact verification.

### [36] [ReSum: Synergizing LLM Reasoning and Summarization with Reinforcement Learning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13316v1)
*Xucong Wang,Ziyu Ma,Yong Wang,Shidong Yang,Hailang Huang,Renda Li,Pengkun Wang,Xiangxiang Chu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出RLVR框架使LLM自我总结压缩推理轨迹，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: ReSum通过自摘要机制让LLM压缩和组织推理轨迹，在RLVR中提升性能并减少轨迹长度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR方法导致不必要的长推理轨迹，降低连贯性并耗尽上下文预算，且现有方法依赖外部机制而非模型自身管理。

Method: ReSum框架：当模型自发触发自摘要时，掩码摘要短语创建对比分支；非摘要位置随机注入摘要短语创建匹配分支；设计感知摘要的优势函数进行对比学习。

Result: ReSum平均性能提升4%，轨迹长度减少18.6%。

Conclusion: 自摘要能有效压缩和组织推理轨迹，提升RLVR效率，模型可自主管理推理过程。

中文摘要：带可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）是提升大语言模型（LLM）长程推理能力的一项关键技术。然而，现有的RLVR方法常常鼓励生成不必要的长推理轨迹，这可能会降低推理连贯性并耗尽可用的上下文预算。现有的长上下文组织方法通常依赖外部机制来组织推理轨迹，而不是让模型自行管理其推理过程。为了解决这一局限性，我们提出了ReSum，一种新颖的RLVR框架，它使得LLM能够通过自摘要压缩和组织其推理轨迹。我们的初步研究表明，自摘要通过降低token级熵来稳定生成，并且引入“摘要”短语可以显著减轻由错误轨迹前缀传播的错误。受这些发现启发，ReSum采用了一种感知摘要的自适应轨迹展开机制，通过对比评估自摘要是否对当前推理过程有益。具体来说，当模型自发触发自摘要时，ReSum会掩码摘要短语以创建一个对比分支；对于非摘要位置，它则随机注入该短语以创建一个匹配分支。我们进一步设计了感知摘要的优势函数以实现对比轨迹之间更细粒度的比较。大量实验表明，ReSum在平均性能上提升了4%，同时将轨迹长度减少了18.6%。

Original abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) is a central technique for improving long-horizon reasoning in Large Language Models (LLMs). However, existing RLVR methods often encourage unnecessarily long reasoning rollouts, which can degrade reasoning coherence and exhaust the available context budget. Existing approaches to long-context organization often depend on external mechanisms to organize rollouts, rather than enabling the model to manage its own reasoning trajectory. To address this limitation, we propose ReSum, a novel RLVR framework that enables LLMs to compress and organize their reasoning trajectories through self-summarization. Our pilot studies show that self-summarization stabilizes generation by lowering token-level entropy, and that introducing a ``summarization'' phrase can substantially mitigate errors propagated from an incorrect rollout prefix. Motivated by these findings, ReSum adopts a summarization-aware adaptive rollout mechanism that contrastively evaluates whether self-summarization benefits the ongoing reasoning process. Specifically, when the model spontaneously triggers self-summarization, ReSum masks the summarization phrase to create a contrastive branch; for non-summarization positions, it instead randomly injects the phrase to create a matched branch. We further design a summarization-aware advantage to enable finer-grained comparison between contrastive rollout trajectories. Extensive experiments show that ReSum improves performance at an average of 4\% while reducing rollout length by 18.6\%.

</details>


### [37] [IterCAD: An Iterative Multimodal Agent for Visually-Grounded CAD Generation and Editing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13368v2)
*Tao Hu,Jiaxin Ai,Licheng Wen,Xueheng Li,Shu Zou,Siqi Li,Nianchen Deng,Xinyu Cai,Hongbin Zhou,Pinlong Cai,Daocheng Fu,Yu Yang,Hairong Zhang,Botian Shi,Xuemeng Yang*

中文摘要：计算机辅助设计在现代制造业中至关重要，但现有的自动化方法主要依赖开环、一次性生成，与迭代的实际实践不匹配。本文提出IterCAD，一个用于闭环、交互式CAD生成和编辑的统一多模态代理框架。我们将任务形式化为多模态代理与可执行CAD沙箱之间的多轮交互，涵盖三个任务：绘图到代码、文本到代码、交互式编辑。为此，我们开发了一个数据合成流程，结合先进的工业制造特征，生成符合标准的工程多视图图纸、复杂的代码编辑任务和高保真交互轨迹。我们通过渐进式SFT和几何感知强化学习（使用可行前缀掩码）优化代理，以提高代码可执行性和几何保真度。最后，我们引入IterCAD-Bench评估套件，并提出Chamfer Distance Tolerance-Recall（CD-TR）曲线及其AUC-TR指标，建立了一个无幸存者偏差的标准，统一代码有效性和几何精度。大量实验表明，IterCAD在多个基准测试中取得了极具竞争力的性能，在代码可执行性和几何精度方面显著优于现有方法，并展示出在闭环迭代优化中的卓越能力。

Original abstract: Computer-Aided Design is pivotal in modern manufacturing, yet existing automated methods predominantly rely on open-loop, one-shot generation, creating a mismatch with iterative real-world practices. In this paper, we present IterCAD, a unified multimodal agent framework for closed-loop, interactive CAD generation and editing. We formulate the task as a multi-turn interaction between a multimodal agent and an executable CAD sandbox, covering three tasks: Drawing-to-Code, Text-to-Code, and Interactive Editing. To support this, we develop a data synthesis pipeline incorporating advanced industrial manufacturing features to generate standard-compliant multi-view engineering drawings, complex code-editing tasks, and high-fidelity interaction trajectories. We optimize the agent via progressive SFT followed by geometry-aware reinforcement learning with viable-prefix masking to enhance code executability and geometric fidelity. Finally, we introduce the IterCAD-Bench evaluation suite and propose the Chamfer Distance Tolerance-Recall (CD-TR) curve alongside its AUC-TR metric, establishing a survivor-bias-free standard that unifies code validity and geometric precision. Extensive experiments demonstrate that IterCAD achieves highly competitive performance across multiple benchmarks, significantly outperforming existing approaches in both code executability and geometric precision, while exhibiting superior capabilities in closed-loop iterative refinement.

Original abstract: LLM-based agents are entering regulated industries where they automate judgment intensive quality management processes. We argue that symbolic structures already embedded in these domains, including regulations, typed process models, and compliance constraints, should be treated not merely as external monitoring mechanisms but as core architectural components that shape the agent's decision-making and behavior. We propose compliance-by-construction as a complementary paradigm to guardrail-based monitoring: a structural foundation that prevents control-flow violations, while guardrails remain essential for catching semantic errors. ### [39] [Uncertainty-Aware Hybrid Retrieval for Long-Document RAG](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13550v1)
*Hoin Jung,Xiaoqian Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 不确定性感知混合检索RAG，可迁移至coding agent的检索增强。

TL;DR: 提出UMG-RAG框架，通过不确定性感知融合多粒度检索证据，提升RAG的生成质量，无需额外训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG中，大检索单元引入噪声，小单元难以可靠检索，需要平衡粒度与检索可靠性。

Method: 利用现有密集和稀疏检索器作为多粒度专家，将得分列表转化为证据分布，通过熵估计可靠性，并融合语义、词汇和粒度置信度；UMGP-RAG进一步用细粒度命中定位证据并返回父块。

Result: 在问答基准上，不确定性感知融合和父级提升提高了生成质量，且保持轻量级即插即用。

Conclusion: UMG-RAG是一种有效的无训练混合检索方法，通过不确定性感知多粒度融合提升了RAG性能。

中文摘要：检索增强生成（RAG）关键依赖于检索证据的质量和粒度。大的检索单元保留了上下文，但常常引入无关内容，这可能会稀释包含答案的证据并恶化长上下文利用。细粒度单元更紧凑，但可能难以可靠地检索，因为短块可能缺乏匹配查询所需的语义、词汇或桥接线索。我们提出了不确定性感知多粒度RAG（UMG-RAG），这是一种无训练混合检索框架，将块粒度视为查询特定的可靠性估计。UMG-RAG不是训练新的检索器或修改生成器，而是使用现有的密集和稀疏检索器作为跨多个块粒度的互补专家。对于每个查询，它将每个专家-粒度得分列表转换为证据分布，从分布熵估计可靠性，并根据查询特定的语义、词汇和粒度置信度融合候选。我们进一步引入了UMGP-RAG，这是一种父级提升变体，使用细粒度命中定位相关证据，同时返回更广泛的非冗余父块以获得局部连贯性。在问答基准上的实验表明，不确定性感知融合和父级提升提高了生成质量，同时保持了轻量级、即插即用的检索管道。

Original abstract: Retrieval augmented generation (RAG) depends critically on the quality and granularity of retrieved evidence. Large retrieval units preserve context but often introduce irrelevant content, which can dilute answer bearing evidence and worsen long context utilization. Fine-grained units are more compact, but they may be difficult to retrieve reliably because short chunks can lack semantic, lexical, or bridging cues needed to match the query. We propose Uncertainty-aware Multi-Granularity RAG (UMG-RAG), a training-free hybrid retrieval framework that treats chunk granularity as query-specific reliability estimation. Instead of training a new retriever or modifying the generator, UMG-RAG uses existing dense and sparse retrievers as complementary experts across multiple chunk granularities. For each query, it converts each expert-granularity score list into an evidence distribution, estimates reliability from distribution entropy, and fuses candidates according to query-specific semantic, lexical, and granularity confidence. We further introduce UMGP-RAG, a parent promotion variant that uses fine-grained hits to locate relevant evidence while returning broader non-redundant parent chunks for local coherence. Experiments on question answering benchmarks show that uncertainty-aware fusion and parent promotion improve generation quality while maintaining a lightweight, plug-and-play retrieval pipeline.

</details>


### [40] [A Three-Layer Framework for AI in Scientific Discovery](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13566v2)
*Guojun Liao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: AI科学发现三层框架，含模型形成与推理，对agent规划有启发。

TL;DR: 本文提出AI在科学发现中的三层视图，强调第二层（定性推理形成模型）是核心但发展不足，并通过三个案例论证其重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI在科学发现中的讨论集中于搜索和执行，忽视了模型形成这一核心过程，本文旨在弥补这一不足。

Method: 提出三层框架：Layer1搜索检索、Layer2定性推理模型形成、Layer3执行优化，并通过三个经典案例分析Layer2推理的结构特征。

Result: Layer2是模型形成的关键，它通过结构性洞察识别框架不足并跨领域寻找缺失概念，三个案例均表现出共同的模式：框架不充分、缺失概念对象、在相邻领域找到解决方案。

Conclusion: 为了促进真正的科学发现，AI研究应重点发展Layer2能力（模型形成与概念修正），而不仅仅是搜索和执行。

中文摘要：当前关于人工智能在科学发现中的讨论通常由两种显见的能力主导：基于现有知识的搜索以及通过优化、模拟和自动化进行的执行。两者都很重要，但都没有完全捕捉到发现的核心行为：模型的形成与演变。本文提出了人工智能在发现中的三层视图。第一层是大语言模型的搜索与检索。第二层作为本文的主要创新，是通过定性推理进行模型形成：识别当前框架在结构上何时不充分，并在更广阔的表征空间中理解问题，不是通过试错，而是通过结构性洞察，了解缺失了什么以及可以在哪里找到。第三层是执行、优化与改进。主要主张是，第二层既是最重要的，也是发展最不充分的。没有模型形成的搜索仍局限于继承的框架，而没有概念修正的执行只会放大现有的表述。我们通过三个案例研究来阐述第二层推理：陈省身对高斯-博内定理的内蕴证明、通过李雅普诺夫函数解决内斯特罗夫加速梯度收敛问题，以及OpenAI在2026年对厄尔多斯单位距离猜想的自主证伪。每个案例都展现出相同的结构特征：一个变得不充分的框架、一个缺失的概念对象，以及在一个意想不到的邻近领域中找到的解决方案。

Original abstract: Current discussions of AI in scientific discovery are often dominated by two visible capabilities: search over existing knowledge and execution through optimization, simulation, and automation. Both are important, but neither fully captures the central act of discovery: the formation and evolution of models. This paper proposes a three-layer view of AI in discovery. Layer 1 is search and retrieval by large language models. Layer 2, as the main innovation of this paper, is model formation through qualitative reasoning: the capacity to recognize when a current framework is structurally inadequate and to understand the problem within a broader representational space, not through trial and error, but through structural insight into what is missing and where it can be found. Layer 3 is execution, optimization, and refinement. The main claim is that Layer 2 is both the most important and the least developed. Search without model formation remains confined to inherited frameworks, while execution without conceptual revision only amplifies an existing formulation. We illustrate Layer 2 reasoning through three case studies: S. S. Chern's intrinsic proof of the Gauss-Bonnet theorem, the resolution of the Nesterov Accelerated Gradient convergence problem via Lyapunov functions, and the autonomous disproof of the Erdos unit distance conjecture by OpenAI in 2026. Each case exhibits the same structural signature: a framework that had become inadequate, a missing conceptual object, and a resolution found in an unexpected neighboring field.

</details>


### [41] [Multiagent Protocols with Aggregated Confidence Signals](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13591v1)
*Ali Elahi,Barbara Di Eugenio*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent置信度聚合协议，通用多agent协作方法，可直接迁移。

TL;DR: 提出三种置信度聚合协议，用于多智能体辩论系统，通过转换和融合原始置信度信号产生聚合置信度，在保持正确性的同时提升区分性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法无法为多智能体系统输出生成或评估整体置信度，且多智能体辩论中的置信度仅用于内部处理，未被聚合为系统级置信度。

Method: 引入三种协议：先转换原始置信度信号使其跨模型可比，再通过软投票或贝叶斯融合（概率融合）组合成单一聚合置信度，并输出最终答案。

Result: 聚合置信度的AUARC显著优于最佳单个智能体和标准辩论基线，F1分数稳定且恢复MAD在模糊任务上的损失；校准提升两种估计器的F1，但对AUARC影响较小。

Conclusion: 所提出的置信度聚合方法能有效产生更具区分性的系统级置信度，同时保持正确性，适用于多种任务和模型。

中文摘要：置信度在自然语言处理（NLP）中用于可靠性、监督以及一系列下游决策任务，但目前没有任何现有方法能够为多智能体系统的输出生成或评估置信度。先前的工作在多智能体辩论（MAD）中使用置信度来加权消息、触发辩论或校准单个智能体，但从未将这些置信度聚合成系统本身的单一置信度。我们引入了三种协议，通过首先转换原始置信度信号使其在不同模型之间具有可比性，然后通过软投票或我们称为贝叶斯融合的概率融合方法进行组合，从而产生最终答案以及单一的聚合置信度。这种聚合置信度在区分性（AUARC）上显著优于最佳单个智能体或标准辩论基线，同时正确性（F1分数）保持稳定，并恢复了MAD在更模糊任务上造成的损失。通过分析两种估计器（序列概率和自报告）以及参数化和非参数化校准器，我们发现校准提高了两种估计器的F1分数，而AUARC对其依赖较小。我们在五个基准测试和四种任务类型上，对每个基准测试评估了六对同质和异质辩论对，涵盖了多种模型能力和大小。

Original abstract: Confidence is used for reliability, oversight, and a range of downstream decision tasks in Natural Language Processing (NLP), yet no existing method produces or evaluates a confidence for the output of a multiagent system. Prior work uses confidence within multiagent debate (MAD) to weight messages, trigger debate, or calibrate individual agents, but it never aggregates these into a single confidence for the system itself. We introduce three protocols that produce a final answer along with a single aggregated confidence by first transforming raw confidence signals to make them comparable across models, then combining them via soft voting or a probability fusion we call Bayesian fusion. This aggregated confidence is substantially more discriminative (AUARC) than that of the best single agent or the standard debate baselines, while correctness (F1-score) stays stable and recovers the losses MAD incurs on more ambiguous tasks. Analyzing two estimators, sequence probability and self-report, alongside parametric and non-parametric calibrators, we find that calibration improves F1 for both estimators while AUARC is less reliant on it. We evaluate six homogeneous and heterogeneous debating pairs per benchmark, across five benchmarks and four task types, spanning a range of model capabilities and sizes.

### [42] [Reward Modeling for Multi-Agent Orchestration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13598v1)
*King Yeung Tsang,Zihao Zhao,Vishal Venkataramani,Haizhou Shi,Zixuan Ke,Semih Yavuz,Shafiq Joty,Hao Wang*

TL;DR: 提出OrchRM框架，利用中间工件训练编排奖励模型，无需人工标注，在训练效率上提升10倍，测试时缩放性能提升8%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MAS编排器训练依赖昂贵的人工标注或子智能体展开，训练效率低且成本高，缺乏有效的自监督评估方法。

Method: OrchRM通过多智能体执行中的中间工件构建胜负对，训练Bradley-Terry奖励模型，直接在编排级别进行奖励建模。

Result: 训练效率提升10倍（令牌使用），测试时缩放准确性提升8%，在数学推理、Web问答、多跳推理等多个领域一致提升。

Conclusion: 编排级奖励建模是提升MAS编排质量和训练效率的可扩展方向，代码已开源。

中文摘要：基于大型语言模型（LLM）构建的多智能体系统（MAS）需要有效的编排来协调专门的智能体，然而训练此类编排器受到有限的监督和高计算成本的阻碍。我们提出了编排奖励建模（OrchRM），这是一种无需人工标注即可评估编排质量的自我监督框架。OrchRM利用多智能体执行过程中的中间工件来构建用于Bradley-Terry奖励模型训练的胜负对。与现有依赖昂贵子智能体展开的MAS测试时缩放和编排器训练框架不同，OrchRM直接在编排级别操作，从而实现高效且高性能的奖励引导编排器训练和MAS测试时缩放。OrchRM在令牌使用上提升了高达10倍的训练效率，同时将MAS测试时缩放的准确性提升了高达8%。这些改进在多个领域（包括数学推理、基于网络的问答和多跳推理）中持续迁移，表明编排级奖励建模是实现鲁棒多智能体编排的可扩展方向。代码将在https://github.com/Wang-ML-Lab/OrchRM提供。

Original abstract: Multi-Agent Systems (MAS) built on Large Language Models (LLMs) require effective orchestration to coordinate specialized agents, yet training such orchestrators is hindered by limited supervision and high computational cost. We propose Orchestration Reward Modeling (OrchRM), a self-supervised framework for evaluating orchestration quality without human annotations. OrchRM leverages intermediate artifacts from multi-agent executions to construct win-lose pairs for Bradley-Terry reward model training. Unlike existing MAS test-time scaling and orchestrator training frameworks that rely on costly sub-agent rollouts, OrchRM operates directly at the orchestration level, enabling efficient and high-performing reward-guided orchestrator training and MAS test-time scaling. OrchRM improves training efficiency by up to 10x in token usage while improving MAS test-time scaling performance by up to 8% in accuracy. These gains consistently transfer across multiple domains, including mathematical reasoning, web-based question answering, and multi-hop reasoning, demonstrating orchestration-level reward modeling as a scalable direction for robust multi-agent orchestration. Code will be available at https://github.com/Wang-ML-Lab/OrchRM.

Method: 构建包含106项评估的EpiBench基准，覆盖CUT&Tag/CUT&RUN、ATAC-seq、ChIP-seq和DNA甲基化流程，通过5,088条轨迹测试16个模型-工具组合。

中文摘要：我们推出了EpiBench，一个用于短时程表观基因组学分析的可验证基准。EpiBench评估代理是否能够从现实工作流状态中做出明确的分析决策并返回可确定性评分的答案。该基准包含CUT&Tag/CUT&RUN、ATAC-seq、ChIP-seq和DNA甲基化工作流程中的106项评估。在来自16个模型-工具组合的5,088条有效轨迹中，没有一个系统通过了大多数尝试：GPT-5.5 / Pi以45.0%（143/318次尝试；95%置信区间[CI]，36.3–53.7）领先，其次是GPT-5.5 / OpenAI Codex的39.9%（127/318次尝试；95% CI，31.6–48.3）。Claude Opus 4.8 Max / Pi和GPT-5.4 / Pi各自通过了39.0%（124/318次尝试；95% CI分别为30.2–47.8和31.0–47.0）。性能在不同检测类型间存在差异，许多失败的运行仍然包含部分正确答案。代理通常能够找到正确的文件并计算出有用的中间结果，但当任务需要更深层次、检测特异性的科学判断时失败。

Original abstract: We introduce EpiBench, a verifiable benchmark for short-horizon epigenomics analysis. EpiBench evaluates whether agents can make well-defined analysis decisions from realistic workflow states and return deterministically gradable answers. The benchmark includes 106 evaluations across CUT\&Tag/CUT\&RUN, ATAC-seq, ChIP-seq, and DNA methylation workflows. Across 5,088 valid trajectories from 16 model-harness pairs, no system passed a majority of attempts: GPT-5.5 / Pi led at 45.0\% (143/318 attempts; 95\% confidence interval (CI), 36.3--53.7), followed by GPT-5.5 / OpenAI Codex at 39.9\% (127/318 attempts; 95\% CI, 31.6--48.3). Claude Opus 4.8 Max / Pi and GPT-5.4 / Pi each passed 39.0\% (124/318 attempts; 95\% CI, 30.2--47.8 and 31.0--47.0, respectively). Performance varies across assay types, and many failed runs still contain parts of the correct answer. Agents often found the right files and computed useful intermediate results, but failed when the task required deeper, assay-specific scientific judgment.

### [44] [AgentBeats: Agentifying Agent Assessment for Openness, Standardization, and Reproducibility](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13608v2)
*Xiaoyuan Liu,Jianhong Tu,Yuqi Chen,Siyuan Xie,Sihan Ren,Tianneng Shi,Gal Gantar,Evan Sandoval,Donghyun Lee,Daniel Miao,Peter J. Gilbert,Nick Hynes,Mauro Staver,Warren He,David Marn,Andrew Low,Xi Zhang,Elron Bandel,Michal Shmueli-Scheuer,Siva Reddy,Alexandre Drouin,Alexandre Lacoste,Ramayya Krishnan,Elham Tabassi,Yu Su,Victor Barres,Chenguang Wang,Wenbo Guo,Dawn Song*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出标准化agent评估框架AAA，对agent设计与评测有通用启发。

TL;DR: 提出Agent化评估（AAA）框架，通过标准化协议实现统一、可复现的Agent评估，并验证其在大规模异构场景下的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Agent评估碎片化，缺乏开放、与Agent无关的统一接口，导致集成困难、测试-生产不匹配和公平比较受限。

Method: 设计AAA框架，由裁判Agent通过A2A和MCP协议进行评估；实现AgentBeats系统，支持五种操作模式；通过开放竞赛和编码案例研究验证。

Result: AAA在12个类别上覆盖298个裁判Agent和467个主题Agent，验证了覆盖率、实用性和保真度；编码案例揭示了之前缺失的对抗性结果。

Conclusion: AAA和AgentBeats为开放、标准化和可复现的Agent评估提供了可行路径。

中文摘要：Agent系统在多个领域快速发展，但其评估仍然分散。大多数基准测试依赖于固定的、以LLM为中心的测试框架，需要大量集成，造成测试与生产环境不匹配，并限制了不同Agent设计之间的公平比较。根本问题在于缺乏一个开放、与Agent无关的评估接口。我们倡导“Agent化Agent评估”（AAA），其中评估由裁判Agent执行，所有参与者通过标准化协议交互：A2A用于任务管理，MCP用于工具访问。传统基准测试定义了两个独立的接口（一个用于基准测试，一个用于Agent），而AAA只需要一个；这产生了一个通用的统一框架，将评估逻辑与Agent实现分离，并实现了可复现、可互操作和多Agent评估。我们进一步引入AgentBeats作为AAA的具体实现：我们确定了五种实际操作模式，使标准化评估与开放性、隐私性和可复现性方面的现实约束兼容。为了大规模评估我们的设计，我们进行了两项研究：一个为期五个月的开放竞赛，吸引了来自12个类别的298个裁判Agent以及来自独立参与者的467个主题Agent，表明AAA适用于异构基准测试范围；以及一个针对编码Agent的案例研究，确认了Agent化评估在保持与公开记录一致性的同时，揭示了之前缺失的对抗性结果，从而产生关于Agent设计的研究见解。通过社区规模的现场研究和受控编码案例研究，我们验证了AAA在异构场景下大规模地提供了覆盖性、实用性和保真度。AAA和AgentBeats共同为开放、标准化和可复现的Agent评估提供了清晰路径。

Original abstract: Agent systems are advancing quickly across domains, but their evaluation remains fragmented. Most benchmarks rely on fixed, LLM-centric harnesses that require heavy integration, create test-production mismatch, and limit fair comparison across diverse agent designs. The root problem is the lack of an open, agent-agnostic assessment interface. We advocate Agentified Agent Assessment (AAA), where evaluation is performed by judge agents and all participants interact through standardized protocols: A2A for task management and MCP for tool access. Conventional benchmarking defines two separate interfaces, one for the benchmark and one for the agent, while AAA only needs one; this yields a generic, unified framework that separates assessment logic from agent implementation and enables reproducible, interoperable, and multi-agent evaluation. We further introduce AgentBeats as a concrete realization of AAA: we identify five practical operation modes that make standardized assessment compatible with real-world constraints on openness, privacy, and reproducibility.
  To evaluate our design at scale, we conduct two studies: a five-month open competition that drew 298 judge agents across 12 categories together with 467 subject agents from independent participants, showing that AAA applies across a heterogeneous range of benchmarks; and a case study on coding agents that confirms agentified evaluation preserves fidelity with the public record while surfacing previously missing head-to-head results, yielding research insights about agent design. Combining a community-scale field study and a controlled coding case study, we verify that AAA delivers coverage, practicality, and fidelity across heterogeneous scenarios at scale. Together, AAA and AgentBeats offer a clear path toward open, standardized, and reproducible agent assessment.

### [45] [EurekAgent: Agent Environment Engineering is All You Need For Autonomous Scientific Discovery](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13662v2)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主科学发现瓶颈从工作流转向环境设计，需抑制有害行为如奖励黑客和高摩擦监督

中文摘要：基于LLM的智能体在自动化科学发现方面显示出越来越大的潜力。给定一个可优化的指标和执行环境，它们能够提出、验证和迭代科学解决方案，并产生了优于人类设计的结果。随着模型能力的持续提升，我们认为自主科学发现的瓶颈正在从规定智能体工作流程转向设计智能体环境：塑造智能体行为的资源、约束和接口。我们将其定义为环境工程：构建能够放大生产性行为（如开放式探索、系统化工件管理和智能体间协作）同时抑制有害行为（如奖励黑客和高摩擦的人工监督）的环境。我们提出了EurekAgent，一个用于度量驱动型自主科学发现的环境工程智能体系统。EurekAgent从四个维度进行环境工程：权限工程——用于有界智能体执行和隔离评估；工件工程——用于基于文件系统和Git的协作；预算工程——用于预算感知探索；人机交互工程——用于轻松的人工监督和干预。EurekAgent在多个数学、内核工程和机器学习任务上取得了新的最先进结果，包括以不到11美元的总API成本发现了新的26圆填充最先进结果。我们开源了代码和结果，并呼吁将环境工程作为开发可靠自主研究智能体的核心研究方向。

Original abstract: LLM-based agents have shown increasing potential in automating scientific discovery. Given an optimizable metric and an execution environment, they can propose, validate, and iterate scientific solutions, and have produced results that outperform human-designed approaches. As model capabilities continue to improve, we argue that the bottleneck for autonomous scientific discovery is shifting from prescribing agent workflows to designing agent environments: the resources, constraints, and interfaces that shape agent behavior. We frame this as environment engineering: building environments that amplify productive behaviors, such as open-ended exploration, systematic artifact management, and inter-agent collaboration, while suppressing harmful behaviors, such as reward hacking and high-friction human oversight. We present EurekAgent, an environment-engineered agent system for metric-driven autonomous scientific discovery. EurekAgent engineers the environment along four dimensions: permissions engineering for bounded agent execution and isolated evaluation; artifact engineering for filesystem and Git-based collaboration; budget engineering for budget-aware exploration; and human-in-the-loop engineering for easy human supervision and intervention. EurekAgent sets new state-of-the-art results on multiple mathematics, kernel engineering, and machine learning tasks, including new state-of-the-art 26-circle packing results discovered with less than $11 in total API cost. We open-source our code and results, and call for environment engineering as a core research direction for developing reliable autonomous research agents.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法忽略科学知识编排，只将论文简化为摘要和引用关系，缺失关键实体、声明、证据等科学推理所需信息。

Method: Agents-K1包含三个组件：多模态解析器（五模块模式捕获全文实体和关系）、4B信息提取骨干（GRPO训练）和graphanything CLI（三源接口）。

Result: 处理246万篇论文生成Scholar-KG，发布100万子集；实验显示在信息提取、知识图谱构建和多跳推理上性能优越。

Conclusion: Agents-K1能有效提升科学推理任务性能，并可扩展至通用领域和符合模式的数据合成。

中文摘要：当前基于LLM的研究智能体通过智能体编排取得了进展，但很大程度上忽视了科学知识编排。现有工作往往将论文简化为摘要、表面提及和平坦的\texttt{cites}边，忽略了科学推理所必需的关键实体、声明、证据、机制和方法谱系。为此，我们引入了\textbf{Agents-K1}，一个端到端的知识编排流水线，将原始文档转换为智能体原生的科学知识图谱。Agents-K1在一个统一的理论基础下整合了三个组件：一个多模态解析器，其五模块模式捕获整个论文中的实体、多模态证据、引用和类型化的实体间关系，而不仅仅是摘要；一个使用GRPO在基于规则的奖励下训练的4B信息提取骨干；以及一个graphanything CLI，一个统一了网络搜索、多模态图谱检索和跨文档遍历的三源智能体接口。在此基础上，我们处理了六个学科的246万篇科学论文，生成了\textbf{Scholar-KG}，我们发布了其中100万篇论文的子集，完整的Scholar-KG可通过下面的SCP链接访问。同样的流水线可以扩展到通用领域语料库和符合模式的数据合成。大量实验表明，Agents-K1在科学信息提取、知识图谱构建和多跳科学推理方面取得了优越的性能。

Original abstract: Current LLM-based research agents have advanced through agent orchestration, yet largely overlook scientific knowledge orchestration. Existing works often reduce papers to abstracts, surface mentions, and flat \texttt{cites} edges, omitting key entities, claims, evidence, mechanisms, and method lineages essential for scientific reasoning. To this end, we introduce \textbf{Agents-K1}, an end-to-end knowledge orchestration pipeline that converts raw documents into agent-native scientific knowledge graphs. Agents-K1 integrates three components under a unifying theoretical foundation: a multimodal parser whose five-module schema captures entities, multimodal evidence, citations, and typed inter-entity relations across the full paper rather than abstracts alone; a 4B information-extraction backbone trained with GRPO under a rule-based reward; and a graphanything CLI, a tri-source agent interface that unifies web search, multimodal graph retrieval, and cross-document traversal. On top of this, we process 2.46 million scientific papers across six subjects to produce \textbf{Scholar-KG}, of which we release a one-million-paper subset, and the full Scholar-KG is accessible via the SCP link below. The same pipeline can be extended to general-domain corpora and to schema-conformant data synthesis. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Agents-K1 achieves superior performance in scientific information extraction, knowledge graph construction, and multi-hop scientific reasoning.

</details>


### [47] [Poker Arena: Multi-Axis Profiling of Strategic Reasoning and Memory in LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13815v1)
*Pratham Singla,Shivank Garg,Vihan Singh*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多轴评估框架和三层记忆架构，对agent评测有参考价值，但非代码优化。

TL;DR: 多轴评估揭示了LLM在战略推理中的能力结构，发现跨维度一致性比单一维度的峰值表现更重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有游戏基准将异质推理维度压缩为单一标量，无法揭示前沿LLM的细粒度能力结构。

Method: 构建Poker Arena平台，结合三层记忆架构（手牌内、会话内、跨会话）和九轴认知剖面，在50个会话（各1000手牌）和记忆消融实验中评估7个前沿模型。

Result: Claude Opus 4.6在筹码上领先（+15,730筹码，14次第一），但平均轴得分仅排第五；持久记忆对不同模型影响不同。

Conclusion: 多轴评估能更准确反映能力结构，标量排行榜存在系统性误排，跨维度一致性比单轴峰值更重要。

中文摘要：不确定性下的战略推理支撑着谈判、金融和政策中的关键决策，但现有的博弈游戏基准将异质的推理维度压缩为单一标量，使得前沿大语言模型的能力结构未被审视。我们引入了Poker Arena，一个无限注德州扑克锦标赛平台，它结合了三层记忆架构（手牌内、会话内和跨会话）与一个九轴认知剖面，将战略推理分解为可解释的维度，例如下注规模校准和位置意识。我们在50个会话（每个会话1000手牌）以及受控记忆消融实验中评估了七个前沿模型；锦标赛筹码和聚合轴得分对模型进行了不同的排序：Claude Opus 4.6赢得了+15,730筹码和14次第一名，但在平均轴得分上在七个模型中仅排名第五，而持久记忆对某些模型有帮助，对另一些则有害。这些发现表明，多轴评估揭示了标量排行榜系统性地错误排序的能力结构，其中跨维度一致性比任何单一轴上的峰值表现更重要。

Original abstract: Strategic reasoning under uncertainty underpins consequential decisions in negotiation, finance, and policy, but prevailing game-play benchmarks collapse heterogeneous reasoning dimensions into a single scalar, leaving the capability structure of frontier LLMs unexamined. We introduce Poker Arena, a no-limit Texas Hold'em tournament platform that couples a three-layer memory architecture (within-hand, session, and cross-session) with a nine-axis cognitive profile decomposing strategic reasoning into interpretable dimensions such as bet-sizing calibration and positional awareness. We evaluate seven frontier models across 50 sessions of 1,000 hands and a controlled memory ablation; tournament chips and aggregate axis score order the field differently: Claude Opus 4.6 wins +$15,730 chips with 14 first-place finishes, yet ranks only fifth of seven on mean axis score, while persistent memory helps some models and hurts others. These findings show that multi-axis evaluation surfaces capability structure that scalar leaderboards systematically misrank, with cross-dimensional consistency outweighing peak performance on any single axis.

</details>


### [48] [Capability Minimization as a Safety Primitive: Risk-Aware Causal Gating for Least-Privilege LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13884v1)
*Laxmipriya Ganesh Iyer,Rahul Suresh Babu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 风险感知因果门控框架用于agent安全动作选择，可直接应用于代码优化agent的可靠决策。

TL;DR: 提出RACG框架，通过因果效应估计和风险控制实现决策门控，显著减少高成本错误，优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有决策系统依赖的模型可能自信但错误，导致高成本后果，需要更安全的决策机制。

Method: RACG框架结合因果效应估计与校准风险控制，建模因果路径，估计反事实风险，推导分布无关的安全界限，并设计自适应门控策略应对分布偏移。

Result: 在模拟和真实基准上，RACG大幅减少高成本错误，保持效用，优于基于置信度和选择性预测的基线。

Conclusion: 明确区分因果风险与预测不确定性可构建更安全、透明的决策系统，适用于高风险场景。

中文摘要：现代决策系统日益依赖学习组件，这些组件的输出可能自信但错误，从而将下游行动暴露于昂贵的错误中。我们引入了风险感知因果门控（RACG），这是一个通过结合因果效应估计与校准的风险控制来决定是否执行、延迟或放弃模型预测的框架。RACG对从候选行动到结果的因果路径进行建模，并根据估计的反事实风险而非原始预测置信度来门控每个决策。为了使门控可靠，我们推导了在高风险条件下行动概率的分布无关界限，并展示了这些界限如何转化为满足用户指定安全约束的操作阈值。我们进一步提出了一种自适应门控策略，通过监测预测结果与实际结果之间的差异来适应分布偏移，当因果假设看似被违反时收紧门控。在模拟干预和现实决策基准测试中，RACG在保持未门控策略大部分效用的同时，大幅减少了高成本错误，并在匹配的弃权率下优于基于置信度和选择性预测的基线方法。我们的结果表明，明确区分因果风险与预测不确定性能够产生更安全、更透明的决策系统，为高风险场景中的可信自动化提供了原理性机制。

Original abstract: Modern decision systems increasingly rely on learned components whose outputs may be confident yet wrong, exposing downstream actions to costly errors. We introduce Risk-Aware Causal Gating (RACG), a framework that decides whether to act on, defer, or abstain from a model's prediction by combining causal effect estimation with calibrated risk control. RACG models the causal pathway from candidate actions to outcomes and gates each decision according to an estimated counterfactual risk rather than raw predictive confidence. To make gating reliable, we derive distribution-free bounds on the probability of acting under high-risk conditions and show how these bounds translate into operating thresholds that satisfy user-specified safety constraints. We further propose an adaptive gating policy that adjusts to distribution shift by monitoring discrepancies between predicted and realized outcomes, tightening the gate when causal assumptions appear violated. Across simulated interventions and real-world decision benchmarks, RACG reduces high-cost errors substantially while preserving most of the utility of an ungated policy, and it outperforms confidence-based and selective-prediction baselines at matched abstention rates. Our results indicate that explicitly separating causal risk from predictive uncertainty yields decision systems that are both safer and more transparent, offering a principled mechanism for trustworthy automation in high-stakes settings.

</details>


### [49] [A Multi-Agent AI System for Automated High School Transcript Processing: Collaborative Document Analysis at Scale](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13916v1)
*Ben Torkian,Jun Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出多agent协作架构，含协调、质量控制信号，可迁移到coding agent的协同工作流。

TL;DR: 提出了一种多智能体AI系统，通过智能体协作自动处理多样化的高中成绩单，实现了96.7%的准确率和每份45秒的处理速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统手动处理成绩单耗时耗力，造成招生流程的瓶颈，需要自动化解决方案以提高效率并减少资源消耗。

Method: 设计了三个专门智能体（模式识别、语义分析、视觉智能）并由编排智能体协调，采用GPA提取作为质量控制信号，实现智能体可靠协作。

Result: 在40份来自13个州的真实成绩单上，系统成功处理所有文档，准确率96.7%，平均处理时间45秒/份。

中文摘要：每年，大学招生办公室都面临着一个巨大的挑战：处理数百万份高中成绩单，每份都有独特的格式、评分系统和布局。这一手动流程造成了操作瓶颈，推迟了招生决定，并消耗了宝贵的资源。我们提出了一种变革性的解决方案，通过一个多智能体AI系统，其中专门的智能体通过智能协调和通信自动处理多样化的成绩单格式。我们的多智能体架构由三个专门智能体组成——模式识别智能体用于特定格式解析，语义分析智能体用于自然语言理解，视觉智能体用于多模态文档分析——并由一个编排智能体协调，管理智能体通信和结果整合。我们的关键创新在于基于智能体的质量控制，使用GPA提取作为协调信号，确保可靠的智能体协作并防止关键信息丢失。在对来自美国13个州高中的40份真实成绩单进行评估时，我们的智能体系统成功处理了每一份文档，与专家人工审核相比达到了96.7%的准确率，同时保持了每份成绩单45秒的实用处理速度。这项工作展示了多智能体协调如何解决复杂的文档处理挑战，为机构提供了一种可扩展的、协作的AI解决方案，在保持准确性的同时大幅减少了处理时间。

Original abstract: Each year, college admissions offices face an overwhelming challenge: processing millions of high school transcripts, each with unique formats, grading systems, and layouts. This manual process creates operational bottlenecks that delay admissions decisions and consume valuable resources. We present a transformative solution through a multi-agent AI system where specialized agents collaborate to automatically process diverse transcript formats through intelligent coordination and communication. Our multi-agent architecture consists of three specialized agents-a Pattern Recognition Agent for format-specific parsing, a Semantic Analysis Agent for natural language understanding, and a Vision Intelligence Agent for multimodal document analysis-coordinated by an Orchestration Agent that manages agent communication and result reconciliation. Our key innovation lies in agent-based quality control using GPA extraction as a coordination signal, ensuring reliable agent collaboration and preventing critical information loss. When evaluated on 40 real world transcripts from high schools across 13 U.S. states, our agent system successfully processed every document, achieving 96.7% accuracy compared to expert manual review while maintaining practical processing speeds of 45 seconds per transcript. This work demonstrates how multi-agent coordination can solve complex document processing challenges, offering institutions a scalable, collaborative AI solution that preserves accuracy while dramatically reducing processing time.

</details>


### [50] [Sorries Are Not the Hard Part: An Expert-Review Case Study of a Semi-Autonomous Formalization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13925v1)
*Vasily Ilin,Brian Nugent*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM辅助的定理证明formalization，涉及agent生成代码的质量验证与迭代改进，可迁移到代码优化agent的验证环节。

TL;DR: 大型语言模型在自动形式化定理证明中能处理局部证明但难以设计全局定义和API，专家评审比单纯编译通过更重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 区分验证定理与可重用库贡献，指出当前自动形式化评估标准不足。

Method: 通过Grothendieck消失定理的半自治形式化案例，进行专家评审驱动的重构和压缩，比较前后效果。

Result: 智能体适应本地机械反馈好，但定义和API设计弱。

Conclusion: 自动形式化评估应包含专家评审，而不仅是编译通过。

中文摘要：大型语言模型通常能够填补交互式定理证明器中的证明空白，但一个被验证的定理并不等同于一个可重用的库贡献。我们通过一个详细的案例研究来考察这一区别：Grothendieck消失定理的半自治形式化。初始版本编译通过且没有“sorry”，但专家评审发现其在定义、定理通用性、文件组织和API方面存在严重问题。随后我们进行了一个受评审驱动的重构和压缩过程，并获得了第二次专家评审。前后对比显示出明显的分裂：智能体能够很好地适应局部的、可机械检查的反馈，但在选择定义和设计API方面仍然薄弱。我们认为，自动形式化不仅应通过关闭“sorry”来评估，还应通过最终形式化是否能够通过专家评审来评估。

Original abstract: Large language models can often close proof gaps in interactive theorem provers, but a verified theorem is not the same thing as a reusable library contribution. We study this distinction through a detailed case study: a semi-autonomous formalization of Grothendieck's vanishing theorem. The initial version compiles with no sorries, but an expert review found serious problems in definitions, theorem generality, file organization, and the API. We then ran a review-driven refactor and compression process and obtained a second expert review. The before-and-after comparison shows a sharp split: agents adapted well to local, mechanically checkable feedback, but remained weak at choosing definitions and designing APIs. We argue that autoformalization should be evaluated not only by closed sorries, but by whether the resulting formalization survives expert review.

### [51] [Minim: Privacy-Aware Minimal View for Agents via Trusted Local Sanitization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13949v1)
*Hexuan Yu,Chaoyu Zhang,Heng Jin,Shanghao Shi,Ning Zhang,Y. Thomas Hou,Wenjing Lou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agent观察最小化的隐私保护方法，涉及敏感性与必要性预测，对agent可靠性和安全性设计有启发。

TL;DR: MINIM是一个客户端本地代理，通过预测UI元素的敏感性和必要性分数，并执行三级披露策略，在保留任务关键信息的同时减少任务无关的敏感信息泄漏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM驱动的自主智能体将完整UI状态传输到远程服务器，导致敏感信息（如认证码、私人通知）泄漏，即使大多数元素与当前任务无关。

Method: 提出MINIM，一个受信任的本地代理，基于情境完整性（CI）学习每个UI元素的敏感性分数(s)和任务必要性分数(n)，并采用三级披露策略（保留、抽象、移除），优化一个对高风险内容惩罚更重的CI感知目标函数。

Result: 在WebArena的真实UI观察实验中，MINIM在减少任务无关敏感泄漏的同时，保留了任务关键的语义上下文和交互可供性。

Conclusion: MINIM通过客户端隐私感知最小化，有效平衡了隐私保护和任务性能，适用于LLM驱动的自主智能体。

中文摘要：现代由LLM驱动的自主智能体越来越依赖丰富的用户界面（UI）状态观察，以在复杂的数字环境中实现可靠的动作基础。然而，许多部署将完整的UI状态传输到远程推理服务器，即使大多数元素与当前任务无关，这可能会泄漏敏感但不必要的上下文，例如身份验证码、私人通知和后台应用程序状态。我们提出MINIM，一个受信任的本地代理，在任何观察离开设备之前，在客户端执行隐私感知的最小化。基于情境完整性（CI），MINIM通过预测每个UI元素的固有敏感性分数（s）和任务条件必要性分数（n）来学习双分数表示。这些分数驱动一个三级披露策略，该策略保留必要元素，在需要时抽象敏感属性，并移除与任务无关的内容。我们优化了一个CI感知的目标函数，该函数对高风险内容更强烈地惩罚必要性错误，从而在保留任务关键信息的同时实现激进剪枝。在源自WebArena的真实世界UI观察上的实验表明，MINIM在保留任务关键语义上下文和可靠智能体动作所需的交互可供性的同时，显著减少了任务无关的敏感泄漏。

Original abstract: Modern LLM-powered autonomous agents increasingly rely on rich user interface (UI) state observations to achieve reliable action grounding in complex digital environments. However, many deployments transmit the full UI state to remote inference servers even when most elements are irrelevant to the current task, which can leak sensitive but unnecessary context such as authentication codes, private notifications, and background application states. We propose MINIM, a trusted local broker that performs privacy-aware minimization on the client side before any observation leaves the device. Grounded in Contextual Integrity (CI), MINIM learns a dual-score representation for each UI element by predicting an inherent sensitivity score (s) and a task-conditioned necessity score (n). These scores drive a ternary disclosure policy that keeps essential elements, abstracts sensitive attributes when needed, and removes task-irrelevant content. We optimize a CI-aware objective that penalizes necessity errors more strongly on high-risk content, enabling aggressive pruning while preserving task-critical information. Experiments on real-world UI observations derived from WebArena show that MINIM substantially reduces task-irrelevant sensitive leakage while preserving task-critical semantic context and the interactive affordances required for reliable agent actions.

</details>

### [52] [XFlow: An Executable Protocol Programming System for Reliable Multi-Agent Workflows](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14790v1)
*Hanqi Li,Jing Peng,Zijian Wang,Lu Chen,Kai Yu*

Main category: cs.PL

Selection reason: 可执行协议编程系统XFlow，增强多agent可靠性，对coding agent直接相关

TL;DR: XFlow是一个可执行协议编程系统，通过将工作流承诺从提示转移到可强制执行的框架结构，提高了多智能体系统的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于LLM的多智能体系统可靠性有限，原因在于缺乏原则性方式来区分提示与框架的边界，导致工作流承诺不规范。

Method: 提出XFlow和XPF，通过可执行协议编程，将非正式语义留在智能体内，将选定承诺转移到可检查、保留和强制执行的框架结构，并使用生命周期管理的符号处理不确定性。

Result: 在约束交互、长上下文推理和智能体软件工程实验中，XFlow通过使约束、证据处理和过程要求明确且可强制执行，提高了可靠性。

Conclusion: XFlow通过明确的协议编程和框架强制执行，有效提升了多智能体工作流的可靠性。

中文摘要：基于LLM的多智能体系统在协调规划、推理、工具使用和人类交互方面越来越普遍，但其可靠性仍然有限。这一局限性的一个核心来源是未充分指定的提示-框架边界。当前系统缺乏一种原则性的方式来决定哪些工作流承诺应保留在提示中，哪些应成为框架结构。我们提出了	extbf{XFlow}，一个用于可靠多智能体工作流的可执行协议编程系统，以及	extbf{XPF}（XFlow协议格式），其领域特定协议编程语言。XFlow位于纯提示编排和标记式工作流描述之间的中间位置。XPF作为一种可读的书面协议，但被编译并作为程序执行。其设计将非正式的语义工作保留在智能体内部，同时将选定的承诺转移到可检查、保留和强制执行的框架结构中。在运行时，XFlow通过生命周期管理的符号来阶段性地处理不确定性，这些符号是具有验证和提交状态的类型化状态单元。智能体输出在被共享状态之前被中介处理，而不是通过提示、转录或隐式记忆传播。我们的实验涵盖了约束交互、长上下文推理和智能体软件工程。结果表明，XFlow通过使约束、证据处理和过程要求明确且可强制执行，提高了可靠性。

Original abstract: LLM-based multi-agent systems increasingly coordinate planning, reasoning, tool use, and human interaction, yet their reliability remains limited. A central source of this limitation is the underspecified prompt--harness boundary. Current systems lack a principled way to decide which workflow commitments should remain in prompts and which should become harness structure. We present \textbf{XFlow}, an executable protocol programming system for reliable multi-agent workflows, and \textbf{XPF} (XFlow Protocol Format), its domain-specific protocol programming language. XFlow occupies a middle position between prompt-only orchestration and markup-like workflow descriptions. XPF remains readable as a literate protocol, but it is compiled and executed as a program. Its design keeps informal semantic work inside actors while moving selected commitments into harness structure that can be checked, preserved, and enforced. At runtime, XFlow stages uncertainty through lifecycle-governed symbols, which are typed state cells with validation and commit states. Actor outputs are mediated before they become shared state, instead of spreading through prompts, transcripts, or implicit memory. Our experiments cover Constrained Interaction, Long-Context Reasoning, and Agentic Software Engineering. They show that XFlow improves reliability by making constraints, evidence handling, and process requirements explicit and enforceable.

</details>


### [53] [Functional Cache Grafting: Robust and Rapid Code-Policy Synthesis for Embodied Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13097v1)
*Saehun Chun,Wonje Choi,Sera Choi,Sanghyun Ahn,Honguk Woo*

Main category: cs.PL

Selection reason: 提出代码策略合成的功能缓存嫁接方法，直接涉及代码LLM agent的生成效率与鲁棒性，对自动代码优化有启发。

TL;DR: FCGraft通过功能缓存嫁接，重用验证过的代码骨架和KV缓存，减少预填充计算，提升策略合成速度和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CodeLLMs在开放领域具身策略生成中存在延迟解码和鲁棒性差的问题，现有方法未解决。

Method: 维护函数级验证代码骨架和KV缓存库，新任务时检索并嫁接缓存，通过拼接和修补合成策略。

Result: 比RAGCache任务成功率提升18.31%，策略合成速度提升2.3倍。

Conclusion: FCGraft有效减少延迟并提升鲁棒性，优于现有缓存方法。

中文摘要：代码编写大语言模型（CodeLLMs）通过将自然语言目标和环境约束转换为结构化控制程序，为具身代理生成可执行代码策略。然而，在开放领域具身环境中的策略生成存在两个基本限制：(i) 由于对长提示重复进行预填充计算导致的延迟解码，以及 (ii) 完全生成式解码导致的鲁棒性有限，通常会产生API不匹配、缺失安全防护和不稳定的控制逻辑。为了解决这些限制，我们提出了FCGraft，一种功能缓存嫁接框架。FCGraft维护了一个函数级验证代码骨架库及其相关的提示级Transformer键值（KV）缓存，并在提供新任务时通过检索相关函数并嫁接其KV缓存来合成新策略。给定检索到的函数缓存，FCGraft通过拼接（将缓存的函数段组合成复合策略）和修补（仅局部调整必要的代码区域以满足任务特定参数和约束，并最小化额外解码）来执行缓存嫁接。通过消除冗余的预填充计算，该方法减少了生成延迟，同时重用验证过的控制结构提高了鲁棒性，优于提示级缓存方法RAGCache，实现了18.31%更高的任务成功率和2.3倍的策略合成速度。

Original abstract: Code-writing large language models (CodeLLMs) generate executable code policies for embodied agents by translating natural language goals and environmental constraints into structured control programs. However, policy generation in open-domain embodied environments suffers from two fundamental limitations: (i) delayed decoding caused by repetitive prefill computation over long prompts, and (ii) limited robustness due to fully generative decoding, which often produces API mismatches, missing safety guards, and unstable control logic. To address these limitations, we present FCGraft, a Functional Cache Grafting framework. FCGraft maintains a library of function-level validated code skeletons and their associated prompt-level Transformer key-value (KV) caches, and synthesizes new policies by retrieving relevant functions and grafting their KV caches when a new task is provided. Given retrieved function caches, FCGraft performs cache grafting via stitching, which composes cached function segments into a composite policy, and patching, which locally adapts only the necessary code regions to satisfy task-specific parameters and constraints with minimal additional decoding. By eliminating redundant prefill computation, this approach reduces generation latency, while reusing validated control structures improves robustness over prompt-level caching methods RAGCache, achieving 18.31% higher task success rate and 2.3x faster policy synthesis.

</details>

Original abstract: The rapid emergence of autonomous AI agents is transforming artificial intelligence from isolated model inference into distributed systems of reasoning, communication, and action. This paper develops the vision of the Internet of Agentic AI (IoAI): an open ecosystem in which heterogeneous agents discover one another, negotiate responsibilities, exchange context, invoke tools, and execute workflows across cloud, edge, device, organizational, and cyber-physical environments. We synthesize foundations from single-agent agentic AI, multi-agent systems, distributed computing, communication networks, game theory, and security engineering to characterize the architectures and mechanisms required for scalable agent ecosystems. The paper examines agent deployment models, workflow lifecycles, communication protocols, interoperability layers, resource-management challenges, and trust architectures, with case studies in adaptive manufacturing and distributed operational coordination. The resulting framework highlights the central research challenges of controlled emergence, semantic interoperability, secure identity, incentive-compatible coordination, resource-aware orchestration, and governance for large-scale networks of autonomous agents.

### [55] [Safety-Contract Graph Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning for Autonomous Network Security Response](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13832v1)
*Jose Luis Lima de Jesus Silva*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 安全约束多智能体强化学习框架，包含预算控制和反事实筛选，可迁移到agent安全设计。

TL;DR: 提出ACD$^3$-GAT安全合约图MARL框架，通过约束优化与预算感知显著降低SOC停机违规与成本，弥补纯奖励学习的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纯奖励多智能体强化学习虽能提升安全奖励，但因缺乏操作纪律而无法实际部署，亟需引入安全约束与预算意识。

Method: 构建安全合约图MARL框架，实例化为ACD$^3$-GAT，分离观测与预算，结合约束优化、图编码、反事实筛选及CVaR风险估计；对比基线包括C-MAPPO-GAT等。

Result: C-MAPPO-GAT将停机违规率从100%降至0.3%，平均成本从355.4降至15.5；ACD$^3$-GAT实现成本48.2但违规率13.8%，位于安全前沿；压力测试显示约束策略退化更少。

Conclusion: 安全约束方法（如C-MAPPO-GAT、ACD$^3$-GAT）能有效平衡安全与成本，优于纯奖励方法，为自主SOC响应提供可行方案。

中文摘要：自主网络安全响应系统有望减少安全运营中心（SOC）的反应延迟，但仅基于奖励的多智能体强化学习（MARL）虽然可以提高安全奖励，却仍然无法部署。我们提出了一种安全合约图MARL框架，并将其实例化为ACD$^3$-GAT（带有图注意力网络编码器的自适应约束反事实决策），该架构将模拟器观测与可重用操作预算、约束优化、图状态编码和反事实动作筛选分离开来。我们在CAGE Challenge 4中评估了该方法，其中智能体在平均恢复时间（MTTR）、误报响应和防火墙变更管理中断的预算下运行。在整个基准测试中，每种无约束方法在100%的评估回合中都违反了SOC停机预算，平均停机代理成本为311-430，而预算为50。这补充了先前CAGE Challenge 4的发现，表明纯奖励学习缺乏操作纪律。约束MAPPO-GAT（C-MAPPO-GAT）隔离了拉格朗日操作成本控制和预算感知筛选，而ACD$^3$-GAT增加了预算上下文、CVaR尾部风险估计、对手信念状态和图反事实风险传播（G-CRP）。重复比较包括IPPO、MAPPO-GAT、C-MAPPO-GAT和ACD$^3$-GAT的三个200回合种子。与MAPPO-GAT相比，C-MAPPO-GAT将停机违规率从100%降低到0.3%，平均停机成本从355.4降低到15.5。ACD$^3$-GAT将平均停机成本降低到48.2，违规率为13.8%，使其位于安全合约前沿，而不是最保守的合规点。拓扑种子和耦合自适应红方进程压力测试保持了这一对比，并表明安全约束策略的最坏自适应退化程度低于纯奖励MAPPO-GAT。

Original abstract: Autonomous network-security response systems promise to reduce Security Operations Centre (SOC) reaction latency, but reward-only multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) can improve security reward while remaining non-deployable. We present a safety-contract graph MARL framework and instantiate it as ACD$^3$-GAT (Adaptive Constrained Counterfactual Decisioning with a Graph Attention Network encoder), an architecture that separates simulator observations from reusable operational budgets, constrained optimization, graph state encoding, and counterfactual action screening. We evaluate the method in CAGE Challenge 4, where agents operate under budgets for Mean Time to Recover (MTTR), false-positive response, and firewall change-management disruption. Across the benchmark, every unconstrained method violates the SOC downtime budget in 100% of evaluated episodes, with mean downtime proxy costs of 311-430 against a budget of 50. This complements prior CAGE Challenge 4 findings by showing that reward-only learning lacks operational discipline. Constrained MAPPO-GAT (C-MAPPO-GAT) isolates Lagrangian operational-cost control and budget-aware screening, while ACD$^3$-GAT adds budget context, CVaR tail-risk estimation, opponent-belief state, and Graph Counterfactual Risk Propagation (G-CRP). The replicated comparison includes three 200-episode seeds for IPPO, MAPPO-GAT, C-MAPPO-GAT, and ACD$^3$-GAT. C-MAPPO-GAT reduces downtime violation from 100% to 0.3% and mean downtime cost from 355.4 to 15.5 relative to MAPPO-GAT. ACD$^3$-GAT reduces mean downtime cost to 48.2 with a 13.8% violation rate, placing it on the safety-contract frontier rather than at the most conservative compliance point. Topology-seed and coupled adaptive Red-process stress tests preserve this contrast and show lower worst adaptive degradation for safety-constrained policies than reward-only MAPPO-GAT.

### [56] [Carolina Guide: A Multi-Agent RAG System with Institutional Guardrails for Academic Policy Assistance](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28360v1)
*Ben Torsion,Jun Zhou*

Main category: cs.IR

Selection reason: 多智能体RAG系统与安全护栏，可迁移到代码优化agent的事实验证和安全控制。

TL;DR: 提出了一个用于学术政策问答的RAG系统Carolina Guide，通过多智能体流水线和安全护栏实现高准确率和安全拒绝，验证了各组件贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在政策指导中存在幻觉和无法强制执行机构约束的问题，需要架构设计来确保安全性和可靠性。

Method: 构建了模块化多智能体RAG系统，包含MMR重排序、检索上下文k=20和引用强制执行，并集成安全护栏以拒绝不安全查询。

Result: 在90个查询上达到98.9%的检索成功率（rel>=2），MRR@10=0.989；安全护栏在30个对抗查询上达到F1=0.89，拒绝86%不安全查询，覆盖93%良性查询。

Conclusion: 生产级LLM系统需要优先考虑安全、透明和部门自治，而非对话复杂性，需重新设计标准RAG模式。

中文摘要：大学生常常难以理解复杂的学术政策，导致咨询瓶颈和获取关键信息的延迟。尽管大型语言模型（LLM）为自动化辅助提供了前景，但其倾向于幻觉且无法强制执行机构约束，使得它们在缺乏谨慎架构设计的情况下不适合用于高风险的策略指导。我们提出了Carolina Guide，一个用于南卡罗来纳大学（USC）学术政策辅助的检索增强生成（RAG）系统。该系统采用带有机构安全护栏的模块化多智能体流水线，为学生查询提供带有引用、基于政策的答案，同时拒绝不安全请求，如课程推荐或个性化咨询。我们在涵盖6个部门的90个查询测试集上评估系统，在>=2阈值（真正相关结果）下实现了98.9%的检索成功率，且98.9%的查询中第一个相关块出现在排名第一（rel>=2的MRR@10=0.989）。通过系统性基线比较和消融研究，我们展示了每个架构组件——MMR重排序、足够的检索上下文（k=20）和引用强制执行——尽管在90个查询下统计功效有限，但仍贡献了可衡量的实用价值。在30个对抗性查询上的安全护栏评估显示，安全F1分数为0.89，正确拒绝了86%的不安全查询，同时保持了93%的良性查询覆盖率。这些结果表明，面向机构策略指导的生产级LLM系统需要重新思考标准RAG模式，以优先考虑安全性、透明性和部门自治，而非对话的复杂性。

Original abstract: University students often struggle to navigate complex academic policies, leading to advising bottlenecks and delayed access to critical information. Although large language models (LLMs) offer promise for automated assistance, their tendency toward hallucination and inability to enforce institutional constraints make them unsuitable for high-stakes policy guidance without careful architectural design. We present Carolina Guide, a retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) system for academic policy assistance at the University of South Carolina (USC). The system employs a modular multi-agent pipeline with institutional guardrails to provide citation-supported, policy-grounded answers to student queries while refusing unsafe requests such as course recommendations or personalized advising. We evaluate the system on a 90 query test set across 6 departments, achieving 98.9% retrieval success at the >= 2 threshold (genuinely relevant results) with the first relevant chunk at rank-1 for 98.9% of queries (MRR at 10 for rel >= 2 = 0.989). Through systematic baseline comparisons and ablation studies, we show that each architectural component-MMR reranking, adequate retrieval context (k=20), and citation enforcement-contributes measurable practical value despite limited statistical power at 90 queries. The evaluation of the guardrail on 30 adversarial queries demonstrates Safety F1 of 0.89, correctly refusing 86% of unsafe queries while maintaining 93% coverage of benign queries. These results show that production-ready LLM systems for institutional policy guidance require rethinking standard RAG patterns to prioritize safety, transparency, and departmental autonomy over conversational sophistication.

</details>

The agent interprets heterogeneous inputs, including natural language messages, environmental observations, and external knowledge, to resynthesize the control specifications. The effectiveness of the framework is demonstrated in an autonomous driving scenario, where the system aligns with personal preferences or responds to social situations such as emergency vehicle yielding.

### [58] [An LLM System for Autonomous Variational Quantum Circuit Design](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13380v1)
*Kenya Sakka,Wataru Mizukami,Kosuke Mitarai*

Main category: quant-ph

Selection reason: LLM agent自主设计量子电路，探索-生成-验证闭环架构可迁移至代码优化。

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个利用大型语言模型进行自主迭代量子电路设计的代理框架，在量子特征映射和ansatz生成任务上取得了优于或媲美现有方法的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高性能量子电路设计高度依赖人类专家，缺乏自动化方法，因此需要一种能自主优化设计的智能框架。

Method: 构建了一个包含探索、生成、讨论、验证、存储、评估和审查七个组件的闭环代理系统，结合网络知识、文献批评、代码生成和实验反馈，利用LLM进行迭代设计。

Result: 在图像分类中，生成的特征映射优于代表性量子特征映射并超越经典RBF核；在七个分子基态估计中，生成的ansatz达到与化学启发和硬件高效构造相当的精度。

Conclusion: LLM驱动的代理系统可作为自动化量子电路设计的可行范式，展示了AI参与科学迭代优化的潜力。

中文摘要：高性能量子电路的设计仍然很大程度上依赖人类专业知识。我们引入了一个自主代理框架，利用大型语言模型(LLM)在明确的设计约束下进行迭代量子电路设计。我们的系统集成了七个组件：探索、生成、讨论、验证、存储、评估和审查。这些组件形成了一个闭环工作流程，结合了基于网络的知识获取、基于文献的批评、可执行代码生成和实验反馈。我们在两个任务上评估了该框架：量子机器学习中的量子特征映射构建和量子化学中变分量子本征求解器应用的ansatz生成。在图像分类基准测试中，生成的最佳特征映射优于代表性的量子特征映射，并且当扩展到更大的量子比特数时，超过了经典的径向基函数核。在七个分子的基态能量估计中，生成的ansatz在满足施加的缩放约束的同时，达到了与广泛使用的化学启发和硬件高效构造相竞争的准确度。这些结果确立了LLM驱动的代理系统作为自动化量子电路设计的可行范式，并说明了AI系统如何在科学领域中参与迭代的科学优化工作流程。

Original abstract: The design of high performing quantum circuits remains largely dependent on human expertise. We introduce an autonomous agentic framework that employs large language models (LLMs) to conduct iterative quantum circuit designs under explicit design constraints. Our system integrates seven components: Exploration, Generation, Discussion, Validation, Storage, Evaluation, and Review. These components form a closed-loop workflow that combines web-based knowledge acquisition, literature-grounded critique, executable code generation, and experimental feedback. We evaluate the framework on two tasks: quantum feature map construction for quantum machine learning and ansatz generation for variational quantum eigensolver applications in quantum chemistry. In image classification benchmarks, the best generated feature map outperforms representative quantum feature maps and, when scaled to larger qubit counts, surpasses the classical radial basis function kernel. In molecular ground state estimation across seven molecules, the generated ansatz attains competitive accuracy with widely used chemically inspired and hardware-efficient constructions while satisfying the imposed scaling constraints. These results establish LLM driven agentic system as a viable paradigm for automated quantum circuit design and illustrate how AI systems can participate in iterative scientific optimization workflows across scientific domains.

</details>

### [59] [Perceive, Interact, Reason: Building Tool-Augmented Visual Agents for Spatial Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12830v1)
*Changye Li,Meng Lu,Yi Wu,Ligeng Zhu*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 工具增强视觉agent，包含tool use训练和推理策略，可迁移

TL;DR: PERIA通过工具增强的视觉智能体，在空间推理任务中显著提升了性能，达到与大型模型相当的水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的视觉-语言模型在需要主动证据获取和多步交互的空间推理任务中表现不足，仅依赖隐式视觉表示无法恢复细粒度空间证据。

Method: 提出PERIA智能体，使用两类轻量工具（感知和交互），并采用监督轨迹合成、复合奖励和OR-GIGPO优化方法进行训练。

Result: PERIA-8B在13个基准上平均提升10.0%（分布内）和4.4%（分布外），优于同规模基线7.0%-14.8%，性能接近大模型。

Conclusion: PERIA有效增强了空间推理能力，验证了工具增强方法的价值。

中文摘要：尽管最近的视觉-语言模型（VLM）展现了强大的多模态理解能力，但在需要主动证据获取和多步视觉交互的空间推理任务中，它们仍然存在局限性。这种局限性表明，仅仅依赖视觉编码器中的隐式视觉表示不足以恢复细粒度的空间证据。我们提出了PERception-Interaction-reason Agent（PERIA），这是一个用于空间推理任务的工具增强型视觉智能体，覆盖地图推理、视觉探测和视觉重建。PERIA使用两类轻量工具族：视觉感知工具用于暴露文本、符号和空间证据，以及视觉交互工具用于操纵视觉上下文、追踪路径和验证空间关系。为了训练PERIA，我们开发了一种统一的方法，结合了监督式工具使用轨迹合成、复合奖励以及Observation-Relaxed Group-in-Group Policy Optimization（OR-GIGPO）以实现有效的多工具行为。在来自8个数据集的13个基准上的实验表明，PERIA-8B在分布内基准上比Qwen3-8B骨干网络提升了10.0%，在分布外基准上提升了4.4%，同时比同规模的前沿基线模型提升了7.0%-14.8%。它还实现了与更大模型（如Qwen3-VL-235B-A22B-Thinking和GPT-5）相当的性能，证明了PERIA在增强空间推理能力方面的有效性。

Original abstract: While recent vision-language models (VLMs) demonstrate strong multimodal understanding, they remain limited in spatial reasoning tasks that require active evidence acquisition and multi-step visual interaction. This limitation suggests that relying solely on implicit visual representations from vision encoders is insufficient for recovering fine-grained spatial evidence. We introduce PERception-Interaction-reason Agent (PERIA), a tool-augmented visual agent for spatial reasoning tasks across map reasoning, visual probing, and vision reconstruction. PERIA uses two lightweight tool families: vision perception tools for exposing textual, symbolic, and spatial evidence, and vision interaction tools for manipulating visual context, tracing paths, and verifying spatial relations. To train PERIA, we develop a unified recipe that combines supervised tool-use trajectory synthesis, composite rewards, and Observation-Relaxed Group-in-Group Policy Optimization (OR-GIGPO) for effective multi-tool behavior. Experiments on 13 benchmarks from 8 datasets show that PERIA-8B improves over the Qwen3-8B backbone by 10.0% on in-distribution benchmarks and 4.4% on out-of-distribution benchmarks, while outperforming previous state-of-the-art baselines of similar size by 7.0%-14.8%. It also achieves performance comparable to much larger models such as Qwen3-VL-235B-A22B-Thinking and GPT-5, demonstrating the effectiveness of PERIA in enhancing spatial reasoning capabilities.

### [60] [Efficient Reinforcement for Visual-Textual Thinking with Discrete Diffusion Model](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14792v1)
*Yoonjeon Kim,Yuhta Takida,Chieh-Hsin Lai,Eunho Yang,Yuki Mitsufuji*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 使用离散扩散模型的强化学习用于视觉文本推理，RL训练方法可迁移至agent训练，但直接相关性一般。

TL;DR: 本文提出使用多模态离散扩散模型替代自回归模型进行强化学习后训练，通过局部视觉编辑提升效率，并采用分解奖励分配解决跨模态干扰问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于自回归模型的方法在视觉推理中需要完整图像再生，效率低下；且联合奖励分配导致跨模态干扰，影响更新效果。

Method: 采用多模态离散扩散模型进行强化学习，利用局部视觉编辑减少计算开销；提出分解奖励分配策略，独立为文本和视觉片段分配奖励。

Result: 与自回归基线相比，GRPO展开计算减少26.9%，性能几乎无下降；分解奖励分配相比联合奖励分配提升11.2%，相比基础模型提升38.04%。

Conclusion: 多模态离散扩散模型是自回归模型在交错推理RL中的有效替代，分解奖励分配能缓解跨模态干扰，显著提升性能。

中文摘要：基于RL的后训练已被广泛采用，以在能够同时进行文本和图像生成的统一多模态模型中实现交错的视觉和文本推理。然而，大多数现有方法基于自回归（AR）统一模型，这些模型在视觉推理过程中需要完整的图像再生。在这项工作中，我们展示了多模态离散扩散模型是用于交错了推理中强化学习的AR模型的有效替代方案，因为它们能够通过局部视觉编辑（而不是完整的图像令牌再生）执行高效的视觉展开。与AR基线相比，这使GRPO期间的展开计算减少了26.9%，且性能下降最小。尽管效率提高，我们发现联合奖励分配（跨模态使用共享奖励信号）会在RL更新期间在无关的图像和文本令牌序列之间引入跨模态干扰。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了分解奖励分配策略，该策略独立地为文本和视觉片段分配奖励。通过分解奖励分配，我们的RL方法相比联合奖励分配提高了11.2%，相比基础模型提高了38.04%。

Original abstract: RL-based post-training has been widely adopted to enable interleaved visual and textual reasoning in unified multimodal models capable of both text and image generation. However, most existing approaches are built upon autoregressive (AR) unified models, which require full image regeneration during visual reasoning. In this work, we demonstrate that multimodal discrete diffusion models are effective alternatives to AR models for reinforcement learning in interleaved reasoning, owing to their ability to perform efficient visual rollouts via localized visual editing rather than full image-token regeneration. This reduces rollout computation during GRPO by 26.9\% compared to AR baselines, with minimal performance drop. Despite the improved efficiency, we find that joint reward assignment, which employs a shared reward signal across modalities, introduces cross-modal interference between unrelated image and text token sequences during RL updates. To address this issue, we propose factorized reward assignment, a strategy that assigns rewards independently to text and vision segments. With factorized reward assignment, our RL approach achieves an 11.2% improvement over joint reward assignment and a 38.04% improvement over the base model.

</details>


### [61] [Iterative Visual Thinking and the Self-Correction Mirage in VLM Grounding](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13156v2)
*Animesh Tripathy,Aswanth Krishnan*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 揭示VLM迭代视觉思维中自我修正的幻象，对agent的验证与自我改进机制设计有重要警示与参考。

TL;DR: 本文发现迭代视觉自校正（IVT）在标准评估中看似提升，实则因oracle选择最佳步骤造成测量幻象；在可部署无标签规则下，迭代无增益，最优策略是不迭代。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将VLM测试时多步推理能力扩展到空间定位，通过视觉自校正迭代优化边界框预测。

Method: 提出IVT：两阶段训练，先利用教师VLM将基础模型自身预测转化为纠正性推理轨迹进行监督预热（无人工标注），再使用GRPO和IoU奖励强化学习。

Result: 按报告方式IVT提升+2.4pp Acc@0.5，但属于测量幻象（oracle选最佳步）；在可部署无标签规则下改进消失，停止于步骤0最优；自验证置信度与正确性弱相关（r≈0.22），循环对渲染框存在而非正确性反应。

Conclusion: 提出诚实轨迹评估协议：报告固定无标签停止规则下的准确率及oracle-可部署差距，避免测量幻象。

中文摘要：让视觉语言模型（VLM）在测试时思考更长时间推动了近期的许多进展。将这一点引入空间定位的一种自然方式是视觉自我校正：模型预测一个边界框，观察其在图像上的渲染结果，并在若干步骤中对其进行优化。我们构建了这种思想的忠实实例，即迭代视觉思维（IVT），采用两阶段方案：首先进行监督预热，其中基础模型自身的预测作为真实误差，由教师VLM转化为纠正性推理轨迹（无需人工标注即可生成训练数据），随后使用简单的IoU奖励进行GRPO。按照此类系统通常报告的方式衡量，它确实有效：训练后的模型在Acc@0.5上比单次基础模型提升了2.4个百分点。我们证明这一提升是测量上的幻象。报告的数字静默地为每个样本保留轨迹中距离真实框最近的步骤：这是一种需要预测答案本身的预言机。在可部署、无标签的停止规则下重新评分，改进消失，最优策略是完全不迭代：在步骤0停止与基础模型匹配，并胜过所有可部署的规则。原因在于验证失败，因为模型虽然能在其轨迹的某处生成更好的框，但无法识别它。自我验证置信度与正确性仅弱相关（r约0.22），反事实叠加显示循环对渲染框的存在而非正确性作出反应。我们将教训提炼为一个诚实的轨迹评估协议：在固定无标签策略下的准确率，加上一个明确的预言机-可部署差距。

Original abstract: Letting a vision-language model (VLM) think longer at test time has driven much recent progress. A natural way to bring this to spatial grounding is visual self-correction: the model predicts a bounding box, sees it rendered on the image, and refines it over several steps. We build a faithful instance of this idea, Iterative Visual Thinking (IVT), with a two-phase recipe: a supervised warm-up in which the base model's own predictions serve as realistic errors that a teacher VLM turns into corrective reasoning traces (yielding training data without human annotation), followed by GRPO with a simple IoU reward. Measured the way such systems are usually reported, it works: the trained model surpasses the single-shot base by +2.4pp Acc@0.5. We show this gain is a measurement mirage. The reported number silently keeps, per sample, the trajectory step closest to the ground-truth box: an oracle that needs the very answer it predicts. Re-scored under deployable, label-free stopping rules the improvement vanishes, and the best policy is not to iterate at all: stopping at step 0 matches the base and beats every shippable rule. The cause is a verification failure, since the model can generate a better box somewhere in its trajectory but cannot identify it. Self-verification confidence correlates only weakly with correctness (r about 0.22), and a counterfactual overlay shows the loop reacts to the presence of a rendered box rather than its correctness. We distill the lesson into an honest-trajectory evaluation protocol: accuracy under fixed label-free policies plus an explicit oracle-shippable gap.

</details>


### [62] [SpatialClaw: Rethinking Action Interface for Agentic Spatial Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13673v1)
*Seokju Cho,Ryo Hachiuma,Abhishek Badki,Hang Su,Byung-Kwan Lee,Chan Hee Song,Sifei Liu,Subhashree Radhakrishnan,Seungryong Kim,Yu-Chiang Frank Wang,Min-Hung Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 以代码为动作接口的VLM agent用于空间推理，提出通用agent设计范式，可迁移。

TL;DR: SpatialClaw通过将代码作为动作接口，使VLM代理能够灵活组合感知操作并适应中间结果，在20个空间推理基准上平均准确率59.9%，超越现有方法11.2个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有空间推理代理在开放性和灵活性上受限：单次代码执行缺乏中间反馈，结构化工具接口无法自由组合操作，难以应对复杂3D/4D空间推理。

Method: SpatialClaw是一个无需训练的框架，采用代码作为动作接口，维护有状态的Python内核，预加载输入帧和感知/几何原语，让VLM代理逐步编写可执行单元格，根据先前输出和观察灵活调整分析。

Result: 在20个空间推理基准上，SpatialClaw平均准确率59.9%，比最近的空间代理高11.2个百分点，在六个VLM骨干上一致提升，无需任何特定适应。

Conclusion: SpatialClaw通过代码接口实现了更灵活的空间推理，无需基准或模型特定适应即可泛化到多种任务和模型。

中文摘要：空间推理，即确定物体在哪里、它们如何关联以及在3D中如何移动的能力，仍然是视觉语言模型（VLM）的基本挑战。工具增强型智能体试图通过用专用感知模块增强VLM来解决这一问题，但其效果受限于调用这些工具的动作接口。在这项工作中，我们研究了该接口的设计如何塑造智能体进行开放式空间推理的能力。现有的空间智能体要么采用单次代码执行，在观察到任何中间结果之前就承诺了完整的分析策略，要么依赖结构化的工具调用接口，后者通常在自由组合操作或针对每个任务定制分析方面缺乏灵活性。这两种设计都为开放式的复杂3D/4D空间推理提供了有限的灵活性。因此，我们提出了SpatialClaw，一个无需训练的空间推理框架，采用代码作为动作接口。SpatialClaw维护了一个有状态的Python内核，预加载了输入帧以及一套感知和几何原语，让VLM支持的智能体根据所有先前的输出，每步编写一个可执行单元格，从而使智能体能够灵活地组合和操纵感知结果，并根据中间文本和视觉观察以及每个问题的需求调整其分析。在涵盖广泛静态和动态3D/4D空间推理任务的20个空间推理基准上评估，SpatialClaw实现了59.9%的平均准确率，比最近的空间智能体高出11.2个百分点，在来自两个模型家族的六个VLM骨干上均获得一致的提升，无需任何基准或模型特定的适应。

Original abstract: Spatial reasoning, the ability to determine where objects are, how they relate, and how they move in 3D, remains a fundamental challenge for vision-language models (VLMs). Tool-augmented agents attempt to address this by augmenting VLMs with specialist perception modules, yet their effectiveness is bounded by the action interface through which those tools are invoked. In this work, we study how the design of this interface shapes the agent's capacity for open-ended spatial reasoning. Existing spatial agents either employ single-pass code execution, which commits to a full analysis strategy before any intermediate result is observed, or rely on a structured tool-call interface that often offers less flexibility for freely composing operations or tailoring the analysis to each task. Both designs offer limited flexibility for open-ended, complex 3D/4D spatial reasoning. We therefore propose SpatialClaw, a training-free framework for spatial reasoning that adopts code as the action interface. SpatialClaw maintains a stateful Python kernel pre-loaded with input frames and a suite of perception and geometry primitives, letting a VLM-backed agent write one executable cell per step conditioned on all prior outputs, enabling the agent to flexibly compose and manipulate perception results and adapt its analysis to both intermediate text and visual observations and the demands of each problem. Evaluated across 20 spatial reasoning benchmarks spanning a broad range of static and dynamic 3D/4D spatial reasoning tasks, SpatialClaw achieves 59.9% average accuracy, outperforming the recent spatial agent by +11.2 points, with consistent gains across six VLM backbones from two model families without any benchmark- or model-specific adaptation.

</details>
